<div class="NavHead" style="font-size: 105%; background: transparent; text-align: left; text-align:center;background-color:#efefef;">Lap leaders</div>
<ul class="NavContent" style="list-style: none none; margin-left: 0; text-align: center; font-size: 105%; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; line-height: inherit;"><li style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0"><div class="timeline-wrapper"><map name="timeline_ef46fb5e43a618df45b887fc4acaf747"></map><img usemap="#timeline_ef46fb5e43a618df45b887fc4acaf747" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/ef46fb5e43a618df45b887fc4acaf747.png" /></div></li></ul>
</div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>2014 Japanese Grand Prix</b> (formally the <b>2014 Formula 1 Japanese Grand Prix</b>) was a <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> motor race held on 5 October 2014 at the <a href="/wiki/Suzuka_Circuit" class="mw-redirect" title="Suzuka Circuit">Suzuka Circuit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Suzuka,_Mie" title="Suzuka, Mie">Suzuka, Mie</a>. It was the fifteenth race of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIA_Formula_One_World_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="2014 FIA Formula One World Championship">2014 FIA Formula One World Championship</a>, and the 30th <a href="/wiki/Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="Japanese Grand Prix">Japanese Grand Prix</a> held as part of the Formula One World Championship. The 44-lap race was won by <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a>, who started from second position. His teammate, <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a>, finished second and <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull Racing</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> came in third. It was Hamilton's eighth victory of the season, his first at Suzuka and the 30th of his Formula One career.
</p><p>Heavy rain from <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Phanfone_(2014)" title="Typhoon Phanfone (2014)">Typhoon Phanfone</a> made the track surface wet and reduced visibility. Starting from behind the <a href="/wiki/Safety_car" title="Safety car">safety car</a>, the race was stopped after two laps and resumed 20 minutes later. Rosberg immediately blocked a pass by Hamilton heading into the first corner. His car then experienced <a href="/wiki/Understeer_and_oversteer" title="Understeer and oversteer">oversteer</a>, and Hamilton reduced the time deficit between them. Hamilton challenged Rosberg for the lead over the next four laps, before overtaking him on the 29th lap and pulling away.
</p><p>The race was scheduled to run for 53 laps, but was brought to an end on the 46th lap (with the result taken at the end of lap 44) after an accident involving <a href="/wiki/Jules_Bianchi" title="Jules Bianchi">Jules Bianchi</a>. Bianchi lost control of his <a href="/wiki/Marussia_F1" title="Marussia F1">Marussia</a> at the Dunlop Curve on the 43rd lap and collided with a tractor crane that was tending to <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Sutil" title="Adrian Sutil">Adrian Sutil</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sauber" class="mw-redirect" title="Sauber">Sauber</a>, which had spun off on the previous lap. Bianchi sustained severe head injuries in the accident, from which he died in his native France on 17 July 2015, thus becoming the first driver to die as a result of injuries sustained in a Formula One race since <a href="/wiki/Ayrton_Senna" title="Ayrton Senna">Ayrton Senna</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="1994 Formula One World Championship">1994</a>. The accident prompted Formula One's governing body, the <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> (FIA), to investigate the incident with a ten-person panel in which it was determined there was no single cause that prompted the crash.
</p><p>The victory allowed Hamilton to increase his lead in the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">World Drivers' Championship</a> to ten points over Rosberg, with <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Ricciardo" title="Daniel Ricciardo">Daniel Ricciardo</a> a distant third. Mercedes extended their advantage over Red Bull in the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">Constructors' Championship</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Williams_Grand_Prix_Engineering" title="Williams Grand Prix Engineering">Williams</a> remained ahead of <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a> in the battle for third place with four races left in the season.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Japanese_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:West_straight_of_SUZUKA_CIRCUIT.JPG" class="image"><img alt="Photograph of the start/finish straight of the Suzuka Circuit in 2010" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/West_straight_of_SUZUKA_CIRCUIT.JPG/220px-West_straight_of_SUZUKA_CIRCUIT.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="161" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/West_straight_of_SUZUKA_CIRCUIT.JPG/330px-West_straight_of_SUZUKA_CIRCUIT.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/West_straight_of_SUZUKA_CIRCUIT.JPG/440px-West_straight_of_SUZUKA_CIRCUIT.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2494" data-file-height="1828" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:West_straight_of_SUZUKA_CIRCUIT.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The start/finish straight of <a href="/wiki/Suzuka_Circuit" class="mw-redirect" title="Suzuka Circuit">Suzuka Circuit</a></div></div></div>
<p>The 2014 Japanese Grand Prix was the 15th of the 19 races of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIA_Formula_One_World_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="2014 FIA Formula One World Championship">2014 FIA Formula One World Championship</a>, and the 30th running of the <a href="/wiki/Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="Japanese Grand Prix">event</a> as part of the Formula One World Championship. It was held on 5 October at the 5.807&#160;km (3.608&#160;mi) 18-turn <a href="/wiki/Suzuka_Circuit" class="mw-redirect" title="Suzuka Circuit">Suzuka Circuit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Suzuka,_Mie" title="Suzuka, Mie">Suzuka, Mie</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> The event's official name was the <i>2014 Formula 1 Japanese Grand Prix</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-formal_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-formal-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> and it was scheduled to run for 53 laps.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Formula_One_tyres" title="Formula One tyres">Tyre</a> supplier <a href="/wiki/Pirelli" title="Pirelli">Pirelli</a> brought four types of tyre to the race: two dry compounds (the white-banded medium "options" and the orange-banded hard "primes") and two <a href="/wiki/Rain_tyre" title="Rain tyre">wet-weather</a> compounds (intermediate and full wet).<sup id="cite_ref-:8_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:8-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Drag_reduction_system" title="Drag reduction system">drag reduction system</a> (DRS) had one activation zone for the race, on the <a href="/wiki/Straight_(racing)" title="Straight (racing)">straight</a> linking the final and first corners.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> The circuit underwent changes following the <a href="/wiki/2013_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="2013 Japanese Grand Prix">previous year's</a> race; parts of the track between the 14th and 15th turns were resurfaced, TecPro barriers were installed on the inside after the exit of turn 15 and lamp posts near debris fences outside turns 13 and 14 were moved back.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Going into the race, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> led the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">Drivers' Championship</a> with 241 <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a>, three ahead of teammate <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Ricciardo" title="Daniel Ricciardo">Daniel Ricciardo</a> third with 181. <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> was fourth with 133, followed by Ricciardo's teammate <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> with 124.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes led the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">Constructors' Championship</a> with 479 points, having won eleven of the previous fourteen races of the season, while Red Bull were second with 305 points, having won the other three races; they were followed by <a href="/wiki/Williams_Grand_Prix_Engineering" title="Williams Grand Prix Engineering">Williams</a> (187), Ferrari (178) and <a href="/wiki/Force_India" title="Force India">Force India</a> (117).<sup id="cite_ref-:1_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes had to outscore Red Bull by 41 points to clinch the Constructors' title in Japan.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Charlie_Whiting_2010_Japan.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Man in his late fifties wearing sunglasses and a blue T-shirt" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Charlie_Whiting_2010_Japan.jpg/170px-Charlie_Whiting_2010_Japan.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="228" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Charlie_Whiting_2010_Japan.jpg/255px-Charlie_Whiting_2010_Japan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Charlie_Whiting_2010_Japan.jpg/340px-Charlie_Whiting_2010_Japan.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1072" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Charlie_Whiting_2010_Japan.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Charlie_Whiting" title="Charlie Whiting">Charlie Whiting</a> <i>(pictured in 2010)</i> suggested to race organisers that the start time be moved to avoid heavy rain from <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Phanfone_(2014)" title="Typhoon Phanfone (2014)">Typhoon Phanfone</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Despite reclaiming the Drivers' Championship lead at the preceding <a href="/wiki/2014_Singapore_Grand_Prix" title="2014 Singapore Grand Prix">Singapore Grand Prix</a>, Hamilton said that he was not relieved because of the closeness of the race. He said that he would take Rosberg's race-by-race approach and was happy to be performing well.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton, who had yet to win the Japanese Grand Prix at Suzuka, aimed for a victory at the circuit.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull team principal <a href="/wiki/Christian_Horner" title="Christian Horner">Christian Horner</a> said that the championship was out of their reach, although he hoped further reliability problems with the Mercedes cars would prolong the battle. Horner ruled out <a href="/wiki/Team_orders" title="Team orders">team orders</a> favouring one driver over the other.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg said he was looking forward to the race, and his car's speed gave him hope for a good result.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Phanfone_(2014)" title="Typhoon Phanfone (2014)">Typhoon Phanfone</a>, classified as a <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_scales" title="Tropical cyclone scales">category-four</a> storm, was forecast to make landfall over the eastern Japanese coast on race day with heavy rain and winds of up to 240&#160;km/h (150&#160;mph). Although the storm was predicted to miss Suzuka, heavy rain from its northern edge was expected to drench the circuit.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/2014_Russian_Grand_Prix" title="2014 Russian Grand Prix">Russian Grand Prix</a>, scheduled for the following week, made it impossible for the Japanese Grand Prix to be postponed until Monday due to freight schedules to Russia for the teams' equipment. <a href="/wiki/Bernie_Ecclestone" title="Bernie Ecclestone">Bernie Ecclestone</a>, owner of Formula One's commercial rights, raised the possibility of moving up the start time,<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> but later said that the event would proceed as planned.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> (FIA) race director, <a href="/wiki/Charlie_Whiting" title="Charlie Whiting">Charlie Whiting</a>, suggested to race organisers that the start time be moved and warned them that the race would not take place unless it was declared safe, but they refused.<sup id="cite_ref-:10_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:10-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Honda" title="Honda">Honda</a>, the owners of the track, reportedly rejected the start time change to allow spectators to arrive at Suzuka in time for the start.<sup id="cite_ref-:18_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:18-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Whiting was also overruled by senior FIA officials, who opposed the disruption of the event's worldwide television coverage.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>There were driver changes for the first free practice session. <a href="/wiki/Max_Verstappen" title="Max Verstappen">Max Verstappen</a> replaced <a href="/wiki/Jean-%C3%89ric_Vergne" title="Jean-Éric Vergne">Jean-Éric Vergne</a> as part of his preparation for a full-time seat at <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Toro_Rosso" title="Scuderia Toro Rosso">Toro Rosso</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2015 Formula One World Championship">2015</a> season.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Aged 17 years and three days, Verstappen was the youngest person in history to participate in a Formula One race weekend.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Caterham_F1" title="Caterham F1">Caterham</a> confirmed that <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Merhi" title="Roberto Merhi">Roberto Merhi</a> would replace <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Ericsson" title="Marcus Ericsson">Marcus Ericsson</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kamui_Kobayashi" title="Kamui Kobayashi">Kamui Kobayashi</a> would drive in the race.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/2014_Formula_Renault_3.5_Series" title="2014 Formula Renault 3.5 Series">Formula Renault 3.5 Series</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Will_Stevens" title="Will Stevens">Will Stevens</a> was announced as participating in the first practice session in <a href="/wiki/Max_Chilton" title="Max Chilton">Max Chilton</a>'s car,<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> but a problem with paperwork sent to the <a href="/wiki/FIA_Contract_Recognition_Board" title="FIA Contract Recognition Board">FIA Contract Recognition Board</a> due to an <a href="/wiki/Industrial_action" title="Industrial action">industrial action</a> in Germany prevented him from driving.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Practice">Practice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Japanese_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Practice">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hamilton_crash_qualifying.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Picture of a damaged silver Formula One car being removed from the track" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Hamilton_crash_qualifying.jpg/220px-Hamilton_crash_qualifying.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Hamilton_crash_qualifying.jpg/330px-Hamilton_crash_qualifying.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Hamilton_crash_qualifying.jpg/440px-Hamilton_crash_qualifying.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4032" data-file-height="3024" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hamilton_crash_qualifying.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> after damaging his car in an accident during the third practice session</div></div></div>
<p>Three practice sessions – two on Friday and a third on Saturday – were held before the race on Sunday. The Friday morning and afternoon sessions lasted ninety minutes each; the third, one-hour session was held on Saturday morning.<sup id="cite_ref-regulations_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes conducted race simulations to see how the cars would behave with a heavy fuel load.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg was fastest in the first practice session with a lap time of 1 minute, 35.461 seconds, ahead of teammate Hamilton in second. Alonso was third-fastest, ahead of <a href="/wiki/Valtteri_Bottas" title="Valtteri Bottas">Valtteri Bottas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Magnussen" title="Kevin Magnussen">Kevin Magnussen</a>, Ricciardo, <a href="/wiki/Jenson_Button" title="Jenson Button">Jenson Button</a>, Vettel and <a href="/wiki/Daniil_Kvyat" title="Daniil Kvyat">Daniil Kvyat</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Verstappen's run ended early when he pulled over to the side of the track at the S curves with smoke billowing from his engine because of a broken <a href="/wiki/Poppet_valve" title="Poppet valve">exhaust valve</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-:2_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:20_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:20-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> while Merhi spun at turn 13, causing Bottas to swerve to avoid him.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the second session, Hamilton set the fastest lap of the day at 1 minute, 35.078 seconds. Rosberg, Bottas, Button, Vettel, Räikkönen, Alonso, Magnussen, Kvyat and Ricciardo completed the top ten.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Some cars went off the track; Ricciardo disrupted the session for eight minutes when an <a href="/wiki/Understeer_and_oversteer" title="Understeer and oversteer">oversteer</a> sent him into a barrier at turn 18.<sup id="cite_ref-:4_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:5_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:5-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Kobayashi lost control of the rear of his Caterham at turn three, damaging his rear suspension and front wing,<sup id="cite_ref-:5_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:5-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:3_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> while Vergne stopped his car on the back straight after exiting the Spoon Curve with a <a href="/wiki/Fuel_pump" title="Fuel pump">fuel pump</a> problem.<sup id="cite_ref-:20_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:20-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Esteban Gutiérrez">Esteban Gutiérrez</a> later lost control of his <a href="/wiki/Sauber" class="mw-redirect" title="Sauber">Sauber</a> entering the Spoon Curve and crashed into a tyre barrier.<sup id="cite_ref-:5_27-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:5-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Vergne stopped a second time with an electrical problem after exiting turn 14; this resulted in a second red flag stopping the session early due to limited time available.<sup id="cite_ref-:4_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg recorded the fastest lap of the third session at 1 minute, 33.228 seconds, ahead of Hamilton and Alonso. <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a>, Bottas, Ricciardo, Magnussen, Vergne, Kvyat and Button occupied positions four through ten. Hamilton drove quickly into the first turn but ran wide onto a <a href="/wiki/Run-off_area" title="Run-off area">run-off area</a> and collided with a tyre barrier, damaging the left front quarter of his car, while Gutiérrez lost control of his car's rear at the exit of turn 15 but avoided a crash.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying">Qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Japanese_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="Man in his late twenties with a head full of hair and wearing a silver jacket. He is holding a microphone in his right hand." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="206" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1890" data-file-height="2285" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> took the twelfth <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> of his career.</div></div></div>
<p>Saturday afternoon's <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#Q" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">qualifying session</a> was divided into three parts. The first part ran for 18 minutes, eliminating cars that finished 17th or below. The <a href="/wiki/107%25_rule" title="107% rule">107% rule</a> was in effect during this part, requiring drivers to set a time within 107 per cent of the fastest lap in order to qualify. The second part lasted 15 minutes, eliminating cars that finished 11th to 16th. The final session lasted 12 minutes and determined <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> to tenth. Cars who progressed to the final session were not allowed to change tyres for the race's start, using the tyres with which they set their quickest lap times in the second session.<sup id="cite_ref-regulations_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg set the fastest time in the second and third sessions to clinch his eighth pole position of the season, the twelfth of his career and his first at Suzuka with a lap time of 1 minute, 32.506 seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-:6_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:6-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-JPN_quali_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JPN_quali-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> He was joined on the <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#G" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">grid</a>'s front row by Hamilton, who missed out on pole position when, on his final lap, he hit the <a href="/wiki/Chicane" title="Chicane">chicane</a> <a href="/wiki/Curb" title="Curb">curb</a> before accelerating too fast into the final corner.<sup id="cite_ref-:6_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:6-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:21_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:21-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Williams teammates Bottas and Massa qualified third and fourth, and Alonso and Ricciardo took fifth and sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-:6_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:6-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Magnussen, whose mistakes on his quickest timed lap cost him time, took seventh. His McLaren teammate, Button, secured eighth and locked one of his tyres—<a href="/wiki/Flat_spot" title="Flat spot">flat-spotting</a> it and slowing his times. Vettel, struggling on corners due partially to Red Bull's use of wet tyres, took ninth. Räikkönen was tenth, encountering problems with his car's balance which prevented him from pushing hard.<sup id="cite_ref-:7_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:7-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Vergne was the fastest driver not to advance into the final session.<sup id="cite_ref-JPN_quali_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JPN_quali-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Because his team had changed his engine, he received a ten-place grid penalty, his sixth of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-ver_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ver-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> This promoted Force India's <a href="/wiki/Sergio_P%C3%A9rez" title="Sergio Pérez">Sergio Pérez</a> to 11th position; he had encountered slower cars entering the final chicane, which forced him to slow and lose brake and tyre temperature. Kvyat's final timed lap was disrupted by slower cars; when he entered the first corner his tyres had not reached their optimum temperature, compromising his run and leaving him 12th. <a href="/wiki/Nico_H%C3%BClkenberg" title="Nico Hülkenberg">Nico Hülkenberg</a> qualified 13th in the other Force India car after he locked his tyres at the final chicane. <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Sutil" title="Adrian Sutil">Adrian Sutil</a> progressed to the second session after making <a href="/wiki/Racing_setup" title="Racing setup">balance set-up</a> changes, and took 14th in its closing seconds; his Sauber teammate, Gutiérrez, struggled with tyre temperature and was delayed by traffic on his <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#O" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">out-lap</a>, leaving him 15th.<sup id="cite_ref-JPN_quali_32-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JPN_quali-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pastor_Maldonado" title="Pastor Maldonado">Pastor Maldonado</a> failed to advance beyond the first qualifying session,<sup id="cite_ref-JPN_quali_32-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JPN_quali-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> but <a href="/wiki/Lotus_F1" title="Lotus F1">Lotus</a> installed a new engine (his sixth of the year) in his <a href="/wiki/Lotus_E22" title="Lotus E22">E22</a> chassis on Friday morning. Like Vergne, he incurred a ten-place grid penalty (carried over to the next race because he qualified within the top-ten bottom positions).<sup id="cite_ref-mal_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mal-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> His teammate, <a href="/wiki/Romain_Grosjean" title="Romain Grosjean">Romain Grosjean</a>, took over 16th position and aimed to qualify higher; however, a change in wind direction prevented him from recording a faster lap time.<sup id="cite_ref-:7_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:7-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Ericsson and Jules Bianchi started from 17th and 18th, with Kobayashi 19th and Vergne 20th.<sup id="cite_ref-JPN_quali_32-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JPN_quali-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Chilton lost control of his <a href="/wiki/Marussia_F1" title="Marussia F1">Marussia</a>'s rear, causing him to start 21st.<sup id="cite_ref-:7_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:7-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying_classification">Qualifying classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Japanese_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Qualifying classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The fastest lap in each of the three sessions is denoted in <b>bold</b>.

<p><b>Notes:</b>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_1"><b><a href="#ref_1">^1</a></b></span> &#160;&#8211;&#32;<a href="/wiki/Pastor_Maldonado" title="Pastor Maldonado">Pastor Maldonado</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jean-%C3%89ric_Vergne" title="Jean-Éric Vergne">Jean-Éric Vergne</a> both received a ten-place grid penalty for exceeding their quota of five engine components for the season.<sup id="cite_ref-ver_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ver-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-mal_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mal-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Race">Race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Japanese_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>There was a large amount of standing water on the track at the start, since Typhoon Phanfone had brought heavy rain to the area.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> The air temperature was 20&#160;°C (68&#160;°F), and the track temperature was 24&#160;°C (75&#160;°F).<sup id="cite_ref-:8_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:8-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> About 142,000 people attended the race.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> The standing water caused heavy spray and impaired visibility, and all cars used full wet tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> The race began behind the safety car at 15:00 <a href="/wiki/Japan_Standard_Time" title="Japan Standard Time">Japan Standard Time</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%2B09:00" title="UTC+09:00">UTC+09:00</a>), with no <a href="/wiki/Parade_lap" title="Parade lap">formation lap</a>; despite the slow speed, drivers struggled for <a href="/wiki/Grip_(auto_racing)" title="Grip (auto racing)">grip</a> on the wet surface.<sup id="cite_ref-:9_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:9-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Ericsson lost control of his car after accelerating out of the final turn, spinning into a gravel trap;<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Motorsport_marshal" title="Motorsport marshal">marshals</a> pushed his car out of the gravel, allowing him to keep driving. Following complaints from Hamilton about poor visibility, the race was suspended after two laps. The cars drove back into the <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit lane</a>, lined up in grid formation and their engines were shut off.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Several cars had their <a href="/wiki/Ride_height" title="Ride height">ride heights</a> raised to make them less prone to <a href="/wiki/Aquaplaning" title="Aquaplaning">aquaplaning</a> on their underbody <a href="/wiki/Skid_block" title="Skid block">planks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:21_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:21-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> The race was restarted 20 minutes later behind the safety car,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> after the rain eased. Alonso stopped his car with an electrical issue – possibly a short circuit from the wet conditions<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> – to become the race's first retirement on lap 3. His departure promoted Ricciardo to fifth place, with Magnussen sixth and Button seventh.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:F1_2014_JAP_Lewis_Hamilton_4968.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Silver Formula One car in the rain; standing water on the track&#39;s surface is lifted by its tyres." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/F1_2014_JAP_Lewis_Hamilton_4968.jpg/220px-F1_2014_JAP_Lewis_Hamilton_4968.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="142" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/F1_2014_JAP_Lewis_Hamilton_4968.jpg/330px-F1_2014_JAP_Lewis_Hamilton_4968.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/F1_2014_JAP_Lewis_Hamilton_4968.jpg/440px-F1_2014_JAP_Lewis_Hamilton_4968.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2167" data-file-height="1401" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:F1_2014_JAP_Lewis_Hamilton_4968.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> won the shortened Grand Prix for Mercedes.</div></div></div>
<p>Although Hamilton became concerned about his Mercedes' brakes, he was told that it was a relatively minor sensor problem. He and Vergne reported that conditions had improved, but Vettel and Massa said that visibility remained poor. The safety car drove into the pit lane at the end of lap 9, and cars were allowed to overtake.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Button immediately made a pit stop to fit intermediate tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton unsuccessfully attempted to overtake Rosberg heading into the first corner,<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> while Vettel tried to pass Magnussen going into the <a href="/wiki/Hairpin_turn" title="Hairpin turn">hairpin</a>, also without success; he then ran wide at the Spoon Curve but remained on the track.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Pérez overtook Kvyat to claim ninth position on the lap.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the first racing lap, Rosberg led Hamilton by 1.3 seconds;<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> followed by Bottas, Massa, Ricciardo, Magnussen, Vettel, Räikkönen, Pérez and Kvyat.<sup id="cite_ref-:9_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:9-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Bottas, Ricciardo, Magnussen and Räikkönen made pit stops to change to intermediate tyres on lap 12. After his early pit stop, Button moved up to eighth place on the same lap. Massa and Vettel made their pit stops on lap 13, Vettel moving in front of Massa and rejoining ahead of teammate Ricciardo. Rosberg made his pit stop on lap 14 and rejoined in second position, 22 seconds behind Hamilton<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> (who recorded fast sector times in an attempt to move ahead of Rosberg after the latter's pit stop). Hamilton went off onto the run-off area at the Spoon Curve,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> reducing the gap by one second. Rosberg reclaimed first position when Hamilton approached the exit of the pit lane after the latter's stop.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> He reported that his car was oversteering, and Button held a 6.5-second advantage over both Williams cars. The Red Bull cars reduced the gap to Massa in sixth by lap 16,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> with Vettel moving to the inside line and passing Massa with a narrow margin at the hairpin on this lap; Ricciardo then attempted a similar manoeuvre on the outside at the Spoon Curve, but Massa accelerated clear heading into 130R corner.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Magnussen made a second pit stop at the end of lap 16 to change his steering wheel.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> On lap 17 Ricciardo went to the outside of Massa on the S-curves and moved inside, passing Massa to move into sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Vettel overtook Bottas around the outside for fourth place on lap 18;<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Bottas then fell to fifth on lap 19 when Ricciardo passed him around the outside at the S-curves. Vettel began to reduce the gap to third-place Button, with Ricciardo driving at a speed similar to his teammate. Bottas was caught by his Williams teammate Massa, who pulled away from Hülkenberg (who went off the track at the second turn).<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Both Red Bull drivers were the fastest by lap 21, but Vettel was still 13 seconds behind Button and a further five seconds behind Rosberg, who now led Hamilton by only one second having run off the track at 130R.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> A dry line began to emerge by this time as some drivers drove through standing water to keep their tyre temperatures down.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:H%C3%BClkenberg_japan_2014_fp.jpg" class="image"><img alt="White, black and orange Formula One car turning left" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/H%C3%BClkenberg_japan_2014_fp.jpg/220px-H%C3%BClkenberg_japan_2014_fp.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="135" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/H%C3%BClkenberg_japan_2014_fp.jpg/330px-H%C3%BClkenberg_japan_2014_fp.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/H%C3%BClkenberg_japan_2014_fp.jpg/440px-H%C3%BClkenberg_japan_2014_fp.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3780" data-file-height="2319" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:H%C3%BClkenberg_japan_2014_fp.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Nico_H%C3%BClkenberg" title="Nico Hülkenberg">Nico Hülkenberg</a> finished in eighth position for Force India.</div></div></div>
<p>DRS was enabled on lap 24. Although Hamilton had closed Rosberg's lead to half a second and used DRS, he could not pass his teammate.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen made a pit stop this lap,<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> which went wrong as his mechanics struggled to install a right-front <a href="/wiki/Lug_nut" title="Lug nut">wheel nut</a> correctly. Hamilton tried to pass Rosberg again the following lap by running in his <a href="/wiki/Drafting_(aerodynamics)" title="Drafting (aerodynamics)">slipstream</a>, but Rosberg held the line and had enough acceleration to defend first place. Hamilton held a tighter line, while Rosberg complained of more oversteer on lap 26.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> On lap 27, Hamilton forgot to deactivate his DRS system and lost control of his rear; his brakes locked, and he went onto the turn one run-off area.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:11_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:11-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> However, he caught up to Rosberg and ran closely behind his teammate into the hairpin without trying to pass.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton moved across the track during the lap in an attempt to pass;<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg's car shuddered, and Hamilton got a better run onto the pit-lane straight. He was in Rosberg's slipstream before passing him on the outside heading into the first turn to take the lead on lap 29.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton pushed hard and pulled away from Rosberg, who lost control heading into the pit-lane straight.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Gutiérrez lost ninth position on lap 30 when he was passed by Kvyat, who drove through standing water on the inside of the pit lane straight and used DRS. Vettel made his second pit stop for intermediate tyres on the same lap, rejoining in fifth behind Ricciardo but ahead of both Williams cars. Button, still third, recorded faster lap times than Rosberg, closing the gap to 12.8 seconds by the beginning of lap 31. Pérez overtook Gutiérrez to take over tenth position on the same lap.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Button made a second pit stop for new intermediate tyres at the end of lap 31; his pit crew also changed his steering wheel, lengthening the stop and putting him behind both Red Bull drivers.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Vettel recorded a new <a href="/wiki/Fastest_lap" title="Fastest lap">fastest lap</a> of the race at one minute and 51.915 seconds, 2.3 seconds quicker than Hamilton. Rosberg made his second pit stop, for new intermediate tyres, on lap 33 and came out behind Ricciardo.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Magnussen experienced understeer and spun 360 degrees after running onto a run-off area. Hamilton made a pit stop at the end of lap 35 for new intermediate tyres,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> giving Ricciardo the lead. Heavy rain began to fall on lap 36; Ricciardo made his pit stop during this lap and rejoined fifth, behind Hamilton, Rosberg, Vettel and Button.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On lap 38, Magnussen ran wide onto the first-turn run-off area, while Vergne went off the track at the second corner and Vettel drove into a gravel trap at the S-turns;<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> all three drivers continued running. Ricciardo closed up to Button on the same lap and attempted to pass him around the inside at the hairpin; Button defended his position, and Ricciardo ran wide.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton recorded the overall fastest lap of the race on lap 39, at one minute and 51.600 seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Weather conditions continued to deteriorate, resulting in DRS being disabled on lap 41;<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_37-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> visibility was reduced due to fading light and low cloud cover,<sup id="cite_ref-:18_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:18-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> while drivers were dazzled by the lights on their steering wheels.<sup id="cite_ref-:19_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:19-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Ricciardo attempted to overtake Button again that lap by taking the inside lane into the hairpin, but Button took a wide line.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Ricciardo finally got past at the hairpin on lap 42,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_39-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> with Button then making a pit stop for full wet tyres. On the same lap, Sutil aquaplaned into the outside tyre barrier at the top of the hill at Dunlop Curve.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:19_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:19-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:16_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:16-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Racing_flags#Yellow_flag" title="Racing flags">Double yellow flags</a> were waved at the corner to warn drivers about the incident,<sup id="cite_ref-:14_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:14-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> and Whiting did not use the safety car.<sup id="cite_ref-:10_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:10-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Sutil's car was extracted from the track by a <a href="/wiki/Mobile_crane" title="Mobile crane">tractor crane</a> that lap and turned backwards toward a gap in the barrier.<sup id="cite_ref-:14_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:14-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Then, on lap 43, Bianchi lost control of his Marussia at 213&#160;km/h (132&#160;mph), veering right towards the run-off area outside the Dunlop Curve.<sup id="cite_ref-254g_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254g-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Although he applied his throttle and brake pedals simultaneously, his <a href="/wiki/Fail-safe" title="Fail-safe">fail-safe</a> system did not work because the settings of his <a href="/wiki/Brake-by-wire" title="Brake-by-wire">brake-by-wire</a> system were incompatible.<sup id="cite_ref-findings_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-findings-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Bianchi collided with the rear of the tractor crane, which caused extensive damage to his car; its <a href="/wiki/Anti-roll_bar" title="Anti-roll bar">roll bar</a> was destroyed as it slid underneath.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> The impact jolted the tractor crane off the ground, causing Sutil's car (suspended in the air by the crane) to fall to the ground.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Marshals moved away from the scene to avoid being struck by Bianchi's Marussia.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Calculations in July 2015 indicated a peak of <a href="/wiki/G-force" title="G-force">254 <i>g<sub>0</sub></i> (2,490&#160;m/s<sup>2</sup>)</a>, and data from the FIA's World Accident Database, which sources information from racing accidents worldwide, indicate that Bianchi's impact occurred 2.61 seconds after loss of control, at a speed of 123&#160;km/h (76&#160;mph) and an angle of 55 degrees.<sup id="cite_ref-254g_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254g-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Bianchi was reported unconscious after not responding to a team radio call or marshals.<sup id="cite_ref-:15_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:15-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Marshals reported the accident, and safety and medical cars were dispatched. Bianchi was extricated from his car and treated at the crash site before being taken by ambulance to the circuit's medical centre.<sup id="cite_ref-:16_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:16-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Transport by helicopter was impossible due to the weather, so Bianchi was taken by ambulance with a police escort to Mie Prefectural General Medical Center in <a href="/wiki/Yokkaichi,_Mie" class="mw-redirect" title="Yokkaichi, Mie">Yokkaichi</a>, about 15&#160;km (9.3&#160;mi, a 32-minute drive) from the track.<sup id="cite_ref-:10_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:10-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A second red flag was waved on lap 46, bringing the race to an early end; the results were taken from the running order at the end of lap 44. Hamilton thus won from teammate Rosberg by 9.1 seconds, with Vettel twenty seconds further back in third. Ricciardo finished just under ten seconds behind his Red Bull teammate, and nearly half a minute ahead of Button. Massa, Bottas, Hülkenberg, Vergne and Pérez rounded out the points-scoring positions. Kvyat, Räikkönen and Gutiérrez filled the next three positions, each one lap behind Hamilton, with Magnussen, Grosjean, Maldonado, Ericcson, Chilton and Kobayashi the last of the classified finishers who were not involved in any incident. Bianchi and Sutil were classified in 20th and 21st, despite their accidents.<sup id="cite_ref-:8_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:8-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton and Rosberg both led on two occasions, with Rosberg leading 26 of the 44 laps and Hamilton the other 18.<sup id="cite_ref-:17_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:17-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton's victory was his eighth of the season, his first at Suzuka, and the 30th of his Formula One career.<sup id="cite_ref-:12_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:12-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;n 1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="After_the_race"><span id="Post-race"></span>After the race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Japanese_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: After the race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Out of respect for the seriously-injured Bianchi, the top three finishers did not spray champagne.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_41-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> At the podium interviews, conducted by the <a href="/wiki/1992_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="1992 Formula One World Championship">1992</a> World Champion <a href="/wiki/Nigel_Mansell" title="Nigel Mansell">Nigel Mansell</a>, Hamilton said that it had been a difficult race weekend and his speed near the end of the race was reminiscent of the <a href="/wiki/2008_British_Grand_Prix" title="2008 British Grand Prix">2008 British Grand Prix</a>. Rosberg called it a good weekend for his team, and congratulated Hamilton on the victory. Vettel said that he was lucky that the safety car came out, and was happy with his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-:11_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:11-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> At a later press conference, Hamilton said that he was confident in his car's balance when he passed Rosberg on lap 28, and saw no difference in the amount of standing water on the track when more heavy rain fell. Although Rosberg's car was set up similar to Hamilton's, he was unhappy with its balance and tried to adjust it during his pit stop. According to Vettel, the weather was borderline and his team decided to make a pit stop when it deteriorated.<sup id="cite_ref-:11_44-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:11-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Bianchi's crash overshadowed the race.<sup id="cite_ref-:12_57-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:12-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> His father, Philippe, initially reported to <i><a href="/wiki/L%27%C3%89quipe" title="L&#39;Équipe">L'Équipe</a></i> that Bianchi was in critical condition with a head injury and was undergoing an operation to reduce severe cranial bleeding.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> The FIA then said that <a href="/wiki/CT_scan" title="CT scan">CT scans</a> indicated that Bianchi sustained a "severe head injury" in the crash, and would be admitted to the <a href="/wiki/Intensive_care_unit" title="Intensive care unit">intensive care unit</a> after surgery.<sup id="cite_ref-:16_47-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:16-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> His family later reported that he had a <a href="/wiki/Diffuse_axonal_injury" title="Diffuse axonal injury">diffuse axonal injury</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Traumatic_brain_injury" title="Traumatic brain injury">traumatic brain injury</a> common in vehicle accidents involving quick deceleration.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> The first family update after Bianchi's emergency surgery was made by his father during the week of 13 October; the driver was reportedly in a "desperate" condition, with doctors saying that his survival would be a miracle. His father said that he drew hope from the emergence of seven-time world champion <a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">Michael Schumacher</a> from his coma.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Marussia also issued regular updates on Bianchi's condition, denying initial speculation about their role in the accident.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Former FIA president <a href="/wiki/Max_Mosley" title="Max Mosley">Max Mosley</a> described it as a "freak accident".<sup id="cite_ref-:13_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:13-64">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Jules_Bianchi_2012-3.JPG" class="image"><img alt="Man in his early twenties with a head full of hair and smiling. He is wearing white racing overalls." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Jules_Bianchi_2012-3.JPG/170px-Jules_Bianchi_2012-3.JPG" decoding="async" width="170" height="235" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Jules_Bianchi_2012-3.JPG/255px-Jules_Bianchi_2012-3.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Jules_Bianchi_2012-3.JPG/340px-Jules_Bianchi_2012-3.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2494" data-file-height="3454" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Jules_Bianchi_2012-3.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Jules_Bianchi" title="Jules Bianchi">Jules Bianchi</a> <i>(pictured in 2012)</i> was the first driver since <a href="/wiki/Ayrton_Senna" title="Ayrton Senna">Ayrton Senna</a> to die in a Formula One accident, nine months after the race.</div></div></div>
<p>Controversy arose after an amateur video clip of Bianchi's crash, showing a marshal waving a <a href="/wiki/Racing_flags#Green_flag" title="Racing flags">green flag</a> at the crash site, was uploaded to social media.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;n 2&#93;</a></sup> Four-time world champion <a href="/wiki/Alain_Prost" title="Alain Prost">Alain Prost</a> said that the marshal should have moved away from the crash scene, but five-time <a href="/wiki/24_Hours_of_Le_Mans" title="24 Hours of Le Mans">24 Hours of Le Mans</a> winner <a href="/wiki/Emanuele_Pirro" title="Emanuele Pirro">Emanuele Pirro</a> said that it was normal practice and anyone who said otherwise was "mistaken".<sup id="cite_ref-:13_64-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:13-64">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> According to several commentators, the marshal committed no infraction.<sup id="cite_ref-:14_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:14-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Former driver and <a href="/wiki/Sky_Sports_F1" title="Sky Sports F1">Sky Sports F1</a> announcer <a href="/wiki/Martin_Brundle" title="Martin Brundle">Martin Brundle</a> called for recovery vehicles to be barred from driving on the track.<sup id="cite_ref-:15_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:15-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Driver steward <a href="/wiki/Mika_Salo" title="Mika Salo">Mika Salo</a> defended Whiting's decision not to deploy the safety car after Sutil's crash, and minimised claims that the race was stopped for intensifying rain. <a href="/wiki/Rede_Globo" title="Rede Globo">Rede Globo</a> lead commentator <a href="/wiki/Galv%C3%A3o_Bueno" title="Galvão Bueno">Galvão Bueno</a>, however, was vocal in his criticism of Whiting's decision, describing it as "the biggest mistake I've seen in 40 years in Formula One".<sup id="cite_ref-:13_64-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:13-64">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The FIA announced a ten-person review panel, composed of former drivers and team principals, to investigate the cause of the accident and published its findings four weeks later in <a href="/wiki/Doha" title="Doha">Doha</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;n 3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> According to the report, there was no single cause of Bianchi's accident; contributing factors included track conditions, car speed and the presence of a recovery vehicle on the track. The report made several suggestions to improve safety when recovering disabled vehicles (which were introduced for 2015), and concluded that it would have been impossible to mitigate Bianchi's injuries with changes to cockpit design.<sup id="cite_ref-findings_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-findings-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Since 2015, for safety reasons, the FIA has required that the start time of certain Grands Prix be at least four hours before sunset or dusk (except for designated night races).<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> FIA safety commission chairman Peter Wright was quoted in July 2015 as saying that a closed cockpit would not have prevented Bianchi's head injuries, and vice-president Andy Mellow confirmed that attaching impact protection to recovery vehicles was unfeasible.<sup id="cite_ref-254g_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254g-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hospitalised in Yokkaichi, Bianchi remained in a critical but stable condition on a <a href="/wiki/Medical_ventilator" class="mw-redirect" title="Medical ventilator">medical ventilator</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He was removed from his <a href="/wiki/Induced_coma" title="Induced coma">induced coma</a> in November and began breathing unaided, enabling him to be transferred to the Centre Hospitalier Universitaire de Nice (CHU) in <a href="/wiki/Nice" title="Nice">Nice</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Bianchi remained unconscious in critical condition there, but his family were better able to visit.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> On 13 July 2015, Bianchi's father said that he was "less optimistic" about his son's chances because of the lack of significant progress and the length of time since the accident.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Bianchi died four days later, aged 25, thus becoming the first <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_fatalities" title="List of Formula One fatalities">Formula One driver to be killed</a> by injuries sustained during a Grand Prix since <a href="/wiki/Ayrton_Senna" title="Ayrton Senna">Ayrton Senna</a> in <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Ayrton_Senna" title="Death of Ayrton Senna">1994</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-cnndeath_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cnndeath-74">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;n 4&#93;</a></sup> Bianchi's funeral, on 21 July at <a href="/wiki/Nice_Cathedral" title="Nice Cathedral">Nice Cathedral</a>, was attended by members of the Formula One community.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The race result increased Hamilton's lead over Rosberg in the World Drivers' Championship to ten points. Ricciardo and Vettel maintained third and fourth place, and Alonso remained in fifth despite his retirement.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes moved further ahead of Red Bull in the Constructors' Championship, with a 180-point lead over the Austrian team. Williams increased their advantage over Ferrari in the battle for third, and Force India retained fifth place with four races left in the season.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<p><b>Notes:</b>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_1"><b><a href="#ref_1">^1</a></b></span> &#160;&#8211;&#32;Pastor Maldonado had 20 seconds added to his race time for pit-lane speeding.<sup id="cite_ref-:8_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:8-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_2"><b><a href="#ref_2">^2</a></b></span> &#160;&#8211;&#32;Jules Bianchi and Adrian Sutil were classified, as they completed at least 90 per cent of the 44 laps used to determine the race result.<sup id="cite_ref-:8_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:8-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-regulations_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_3"><b><a href="#ref_3">^3</a></b></span> &#160;&#8211;&#32;Jules Bianchi died on 17 July 2015 from injuries sustained during the accident.<sup id="cite_ref-cnndeath_74-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cnndeath-74">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes_and_references">Notes and references</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Japanese_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Notes and references">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Japanese_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-59"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-59">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Hamilton had previously won in Japan at the <a href="/wiki/Fuji_Speedway" title="Fuji Speedway">Fuji Speedway</a> in <a href="/wiki/2007_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="2007 Japanese Grand Prix">2007</a> while driving for McLaren.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-65"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-65">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The video, recorded by a spectator in a nearby grandstand, was removed from social media sites upon the orders of <a href="/wiki/Formula_One_Group" title="Formula One Group">Formula One Management</a> officials. As of 2019, the company has not released any official video footage of the accident.<sup id="cite_ref-:13_64-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:13-64">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-67"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-67">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"> The panel was led by the FIA's safety commission president Peter Wright and included former team principals <a href="/wiki/Ross_Brawn" title="Ross Brawn">Ross Brawn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stefano_Domenicali" title="Stefano Domenicali">Stefano Domenicali</a>, chief stewards' representative Gerd Ennser, FIA drivers' commission president <a href="/wiki/Emerson_Fittipaldi" title="Emerson Fittipaldi">Emerson Fittipaldi</a>, <a href="/wiki/FIA_World_Endurance_Championship" title="FIA World Endurance Championship">World Endurance Championship</a> race director Eduardo Freitas, the circuits commission president, Roger Peart, Antonio Rigozzi, judge at the FIA's International Court of Appeal, the FIA institute and medical commission president, Gérard Saillant, and the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Prix_Drivers%27_Association" title="Grand Prix Drivers&#39; Association">Grand Prix Drivers' Association</a> president, <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Wurz" title="Alexander Wurz">Alexander Wurz</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-76"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-76">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Bianchi's granduncle, <a href="/wiki/Lucien_Bianchi" title="Lucien Bianchi">Lucien</a>, was killed in a crash during a test session at the <a href="/wiki/Circuit_de_la_Sarthe" title="Circuit de la Sarthe">Circuit de la Sarthe</a> in 1969.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
</ol></div>
